             <div class="views-field views-field-field-slide-image">
              <div class="field-content">
               <div class="slide-image-container" style="background-image: url('http://www.mentalhealthamerica.net/sites/default/files/styles/home_slide/public/images/home-slides/2018_mha_mhm_homepage_slide.png?itok=7NHwOOPt');">

             <div class="views-field views-field-nothing">
              <span class="field-content">
               <div class="slide-caption">
                <div class="slide-caption-text">
                 <h3>
                  May is Mental Health Month 2018
                 </h3>
                 <p>
                  May is right around the corner. Start planning.
                 </p>
